// These are base actors for monsters, miscellaneous characters,
// and other actors that require them for one reason or another.
// They are split into 8 possible types with 5 sizes, or 40 total bases

// Humanoid enemies

Actor Samsara_BossDeath : Trigger
{
	States
	{
		Pickup:
			TNT1 A 0 A_BossDeath
			Stop
	}
}

Actor Samsara_KillMaster : Trigger
{
	States
	{
		Pickup:
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			Stop
	}
}
